<script type="text/javascript">
  var button = document.getElementById("dropdownLabel");

  var openDropdown = function() {

    var myDropdown = document.getElementById("dropdownMenu");
    var button = document.getElementById("dropdownLabel");

    myDropdown.classList.add('Header__dropdownMenuOpen');
    button.removeEventListener('click', openDropdown);
    document.body.addEventListener('click', closeDropdown, true);
  };

var closeDropdown = function() {
  var myDropdown = document.getElementById("dropdownMenu");
  var button = document.getElementById("dropdownLabel");

  myDropdown.classList.remove('Header__dropdownMenuOpen');
  document.body.removeEventListener('click', closeDropdown);
  button.addEventListener('click', openDropdown, true);
};

button.addEventListener('click', openDropdown);

</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
  var button = document.getElementById("dropdownLabelAccount");

  var openDropdownAccount = function() {
    var myDropdown = document.getElementById("dropdownMenuAccount");
    var button = document.getElementById("dropdownLabelAccount");

    myDropdown.classList.add('Header__dropdownMenuOpen');
    button.classList.add("Header__dropdownLabelOpen");
    button.removeEventListener('click', openDropdownAccount);
    document.body.addEventListener('click', closeDropdownAccount, true);
  };

  var closeDropdownAccount = function() {
    var myDropdown = document.getElementById("dropdownMenuAccount");
    var button = document.getElementById("dropdownLabelAccount");

    myDropdown.classList.remove('Header__dropdownMenuOpen');
    button.classList.remove("Header__dropdownLabelOpen");

    document.body.removeEventListener('click', closeDropdownAccount);
    button.addEventListener('click', openDropdownAccount, true);
  };

button.addEventListener('click', openDropdownAccount);

</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
var eventMethod = window.addEventListener ? 'addEventListener' : 'attachEvent';
var messageEvent = eventMethod === 'attachEvent' ? 'onmessage' : 'message';
var eventer = window[eventMethod];
function receiveOptInMessage(event) {
  function eventDataContains(str) {
    return JSON.stringify(event.data).indexOf(str) !== -1;
  }
  if (event && event.data && (eventDataContains('oil_optin_done'))) {
    if (window.ga && window.ga.loaded) {
        window.ga('send', 'event', 'CMP', 'oil_optin_done', {'nonInteraction': true});
        window.__cmp('getPublisherConsents', null, function(result){
          var choice1 = result.standardPurposeConsents[1];
          var choice2 = result.standardPurposeConsents[2];
          var choice3 = result.standardPurposeConsents[3];
          var choice4 = result.standardPurposeConsents[4];
          var choice5 = result.standardPurposeConsents[5];
          window.ga('send', 'event', 'CMP', 'Consent', 'Information storage and access', choice1, {'nonInteraction': true});
          window.ga('send', 'event', 'CMP', 'Consent', 'Personalisation', choice2, {'nonInteraction': true});
          window.ga('send', 'event', 'CMP', 'Consent', 'Ad selection, delivery, reporting', choice3, {'nonInteraction': true});
          window.ga('send', 'event', 'CMP', 'Consent', 'Content selection, delivery, reporting', choice4, {'nonInteraction': true});
          window.ga('send', 'event', 'CMP', 'Consent', 'Measurement', choice5, {'nonInteraction': true});
          window.ga('send', 'event', 'CMP', 'Consent', 'All', choice1&&choice2&&choice3&&choice4&&choice5, {'nonInteraction': true});
        });
    }
  }
}
eventer(messageEvent, receiveOptInMessage, false);

<script type="text/javascript">
  var button = document.getElementById("dropdownLabel");

  var openDropdown = function() {

    var myDropdown = document.getElementById("dropdownMenu");
    var button = document.getElementById("dropdownLabel");

    myDropdown.classList.add('Header__dropdownMenuOpen');
    button.removeEventListener('click', openDropdown);
    document.body.addEventListener('click', closeDropdown, true);
  };

var closeDropdown = function() {
  var myDropdown = document.getElementById("dropdownMenu");
  var button = document.getElementById("dropdownLabel");

  myDropdown.classList.remove('Header__dropdownMenuOpen');
  document.body.removeEventListener('click', closeDropdown);
  button.addEventListener('click', openDropdown, true);
};

button.addEventListener('click', openDropdown);

</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
  var button = document.getElementById("dropdownLabelAccount");

  var openDropdownAccount = function() {
    var myDropdown = document.getElementById("dropdownMenuAccount");
    var button = document.getElementById("dropdownLabelAccount");

    myDropdown.classList.add('Header__dropdownMenuOpen');
    button.classList.add("Header__dropdownLabelOpen");
    button.removeEventListener('click', openDropdownAccount);
    document.body.addEventListener('click', closeDropdownAccount, true);
  };

  var closeDropdownAccount = function() {
    var myDropdown = document.getElementById("dropdownMenuAccount");
    var button = document.getElementById("dropdownLabelAccount");

    myDropdown.classList.remove('Header__dropdownMenuOpen');
    button.classList.remove("Header__dropdownLabelOpen");

    document.body.removeEventListener('click', closeDropdownAccount);
    button.addEventListener('click', openDropdownAccount, true);
  };

button.addEventListener('click', openDropdownAccount);

</script>
